data-v-88cd4b9c="">Sony BDP-S6700 specifications</h2><p data-v-88cd4b9c="">Below you will find the product specifications and the manual specifications of the Sony BDP-S6700.</p><p style="white-space:pre-wrap;" data-v-88cd4b9c="">The Sony BDP-S6700 is a firmware upgradeable blu-ray player that offers various features for an enhanced viewing experience. With its child lock and parental control options, users can ensure a safe and appropriate entertainment environment for their children.

This blu-ray player supports multiple disc types, including BD, CD, and DVD, allowing users to easily enjoy a wide range of media. However, it does not have an integrated card reader for additional convenience.

One notable feature of the Sony BDP-S6700 is its smartphone remote support, allowing users to control the player through their smartphones. Additionally, LED indicators provide visual feedback, indicating the player's status and operation.

The Sony BDP-S6700 boasts 3D capability for an immersive viewing experience. With an HDMI port, users can easily connect the blu-ray player to their high-definition televisions or other compatible devices. It also features an Ethernet LAN port for seamless connectivity.

Equipped with a USB 2.0 port, this blu-ray player offers additional convenience by allowing users to connect and play their media directly from compatible external devices. Furthermore, it supports Full HD resolution, ensuring crisp and clear visuals.

In conclusion, the Sony BDP-S6700 is a firmware upgradeable blu-ray player that supports various disc types. Its smartphone remote support, LED indicators, and 3D capability contribute to an improved entertainment experience. With HDMI, USB, and Ethernet connectivity options, this blu-ray player provides versatility and convenience for users seeking a reliable and high-quality media player.</p><div class="feature-logos
